# Stage fastqc [HS1250_A]
fastqc -o 01_fastqc --noextract -f fastq /scratch/alauring_fluxm/mccrone/HIVE/data/raw/HK_6/HS1250_A.1.1.fastq
fastqc -o 01_fastqc --noextract -f fastq /scratch/alauring_fluxm/mccrone/HIVE/data/raw/HK_6/HS1250_A.2.1.fastq
# Stage bowtie2 [HS1250_A]
bowtie2 --seed 42 --sensitive -x /scratch/alauring_fluxm/mccrone/HIVE/data/reference/Hong_Kong_PC1A -1 /scratch/alauring_fluxm/mccrone/HIVE/data/raw/HK_6/HS1250_A.1.1.fastq -2 /scratch/alauring_fluxm/mccrone/HIVE/data/raw/HK_6/HS1250_A.2.1.fastq -S ./03_align/HS1250_A.sam 2> ./03_align/HS1250_A.log
# Stage picard_sortsam [HS1250_A]
java -Xmx4g -Djava.io.tmpdir=./tmp -jar /home/mccrone/variant_pipeline/lib/picard-tools-1.133/picard.jar SortSam SO=coordinate INPUT=./03_align/HS1250_A.sam OUTPUT=03_align/HS1250_A.bam VALIDATION_STRINGENCY=LENIENT CREATE_INDEX=true
# Stage picard_removedups [HS1250_A]
java -Xmx2g -Djava.io.tmpdir=./tmp -jar /home/mccrone/variant_pipeline/lib/picard-tools-1.133/picard.jar MarkDuplicates INPUT=03_align/HS1250_A.bam OUTPUT=04_removed_duplicates/HS1250_A.removed.bam REMOVE_DUPLICATES=true CREATE_INDEX=true METRICS_FILE=04_removed_duplicates/HS1250_A.removed.bam-picard.out.metrics VALIDATION_STRINGENCY=LENIENT
# Stage get_control
# Stage deepsnv [HS1250_A]
Rscript  /home/mccrone/variant_pipeline/scripts/deepSNV.R /scratch/alauring_fluxm/mccrone/HIVE/data/reference/Hong_Kong_PC1A.fa 04_removed_duplicates/HS1250_A.removed.bam 04_removed_duplicates/PC1A.removed.bam bonferroni 0.1 fisher two.sided 0.5 deepSNV/HS1250_A.removed.csv deepSNV/HS1250_A.removed.fasta
